## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Compliance Audit: Envoy Access Logging Configuration Coverage

## Your Task

Audit the access logging infrastructure in `envoyproxy/envoy`. Find all C++ source files under `source/extensions/access_loggers/` and `source/common/access_log/` that define access log filter implementations or access log sink implementations. Also find the corresponding `.proto` definitions in `envoyproxy/data-plane-api` under `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/`. For each implementation, report whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],

    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've completed the comprehensive audit of Envoy's access logging infrastructure. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Audit Summary

I've analyzed the Envoy v1.31.2 access logging infrastructure and created a detailed report at `/workspace/answer.json` covering:

### **Access Log Sink Implementations Found:**

1. **File Access Logger** - ✅ FULL JSON SUPPORT
   - Multiple JSON format options (json_format, typed_json_format, SubstitutionFormatString)
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/`

2. **Stream Access Loggers (stdout/stderr)** - ✅ SUPPORTS JSON
   - Uses SubstitutionFormatString for flexible formatting
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/`

3. **Fluentd Access Logger** - ✅ STRUCTURED JSON
   - Creates structured JSON, converts to MessagePack for Fluentd protocol
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/`

4. **gRPC Access Logger (HTTP & TCP)** - ❌ BINARY PROTOBUF
   - Sends structured protobuf messages (HTTPAccessLogEntry, TCPAccessLogEntry)
   - Not JSON or text format
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/`

5. **OpenTelemetry Access Logger** - ❌ BINARY OTEL PROTOBUF
   - Sends OpenTelemetry Log Resource messages in binary format
   - Not JSON or text format
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/`

6. **WASM Access Logger** - ⚠️ IMPLEMENTATION-DEPENDENT
   - Format depends on WASM module implementation
   - Located in `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/`

### **Filters and Proto-Only Implementations:**
- CEL Expression Filter (filter implementation, not a sink)
- Process Rate Limit Filter (filter implementation, not a sink)
- Dynamic Modules (proto defined but no C++ implementation in v1.31.2)
- Stats Access Logger (proto defined but no C++ implementat
